Quick Look Log

The Skynet/NRAO 20m regularly observes bright point sources and also produces maps of interesting regions of the Sky. This web page links to Quick-Look Maps of the most recent observations.
Skynet website home is: http://skynet.unc.edu
GB 20-meter info: http://www.gb.nrao.edu/20m
Latest Obs: latest obs

Jump to end

Note: observations before Feb 1, 2013 have been moved to /raid/scratch/cyborg/webback_02_2013 -- ask F. Ghigo if you want to retrieve any data from before that.
